route-policy rpToBR
  if destination in plDefaultRoute then
    set med 10000
    set next-hop self
    pass
  elseif destination in plTo163 then
    drop
  elseif as-path in (ios-regex '^$') then
    pass
  elseif as-path in privateAS then
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy rpToCR
  if destination in plTo163 then
    set med 0
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy rpTo163
  if destination in plTo163 then
    set med 5
    set community N-169 additive
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy rpToCN2
  if destination in plTo163 then
    set med 0
    set community 163 additive
    pass
  elseif destination in plToCN2 then
    set med 0
    set community CN2 additive
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!

  if (destination in plTo163) then
    pass
  elseif (as-path in (ios-regex '^$')) then
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
